40 CCUBRIDDataSource *CCUBRIDRowset::GetDataSourcePtr()
41 {
42  return GetSessionPtr()->GetDataSourcePtr();
43 }

45 CCUBRIDSession *CCUBRIDRowset::GetSessionPtr()
46 {
47  switch(m_eType)
48  {
49  case FromSession:
50  return CCUBRIDSession::GetSessionPtr(this);
51  case FromCommand:
52  return GetCommandPtr()->GetSessionPtr();
53  case FromRow:
54  return NULL; // TODO
55  default: // Invalid
56  return NULL;
57  }
58 }

60 CCUBRIDCommand *CCUBRIDRowset::GetCommandPtr()
61 {
62  return CCUBRIDCommand::GetCommandPtr(this);
63 }

65 CCUBRIDRowset *CCUBRIDRowset::GetRowsetPtr(IObjectWithSite *pSite)
66 {
67  CComPtr<IRowset> spCom;
68  HRESULT hr = pSite->GetSite(__uuidof(IRowset), (void **)&spCom);
69  // 제대로 프로그래밍 됐을때, 실패하는 경우가 있을까?
70  ATLASSERT(SUCCEEDED(hr));
71  // 굳이 오버헤드를 감수해가며 dynamic_cast를 쓸 필요는 없을 듯 return static_cast<CCUBRIDRowset *>((IRowset *)spCom); } HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::GetConnectionHandle(int *phConn) { return GetSessionPtr()->GetConnectionHandle(phConn); } int CCUBRIDRowset::GetRequestHandle() { switch(m_eType) { case FromSession: return m_hReq; case FromCommand: return GetCommandPtr()->m_hReq; case FromRow: return 0; // TODO default: // Invalid return 0; } } CCUBRIDRowset::CCUBRIDRowset() : m_eType(Invalid), m_hReq(0), m_bAsynch(false), m_nStatus(0), m_bFindForward(true) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "CCUBRIDRowset::CCUBRIDRowset\n"); // RegisterTxnCallback은 m_eType이 정해진 후에야 가능하다. } CCUBRIDRowset::~CCUBRIDRowset() { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "CCUBRIDRowset::~CCUBRIDRowset\n"); CCUBRIDSession *pSession = GetSessionPtr(); if(pSession) { //pSession->RowsetCommit(); #if 1 if(m_bIsChangeable) pSession->RowsetCommit(); #endif pSession->RegisterTxnCallback(this, false); } } HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::ValidateCommandID(DBID *pTableID, DBID *pIndexID) { HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::ValidateCommandID(pTableID, pIndexID); if (hr != S_OK) return hr; if(pIndexID) return RaiseError(DB_E_NOINDEX, 0, __uuidof(IOpenRowset)); // 인덱스를 지원하지 않는다. if(pTableID && (pTableID->uName.pwszName==NULL || wcslen(pTableID->uName.pwszName)==0)) return RaiseError(DB_E_NOTABLE, 0, __uuidof(IOpenRowset)); // 테이블 이름이 없다. return S_OK; } // cci_fetch_size를 설정한다. static HRESULT SetFetchSize(CCUBRIDRowset *pRowset) { CCUBRIDDataSource *pDS = pRowset->GetDataSourcePtr(); CComVariant var; pDS->GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_UNIPROVIDER_DBINIT, DBPROP_UNIPROVIDER_FETCH_SIZE, &var); int rc = cci_fetch_size(pRowset->GetRequestHandle(), V_I4(&var)); if(rc<0) RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "Failed to set the fetch size"); return S_OK; } HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::InitCommon(int cResult, bool bRegist) { m_rgRowData.SetCount(cResult); // 1과 2는 DBBMK_FIRST, DBBMK_LAST를 위해 비워놓는다. // cbBookmark가 1과 4로 다르긴 한데 // IRowsetLocateImpl은 구현이 잘못되서 구별을 잘 못한다. m_rgBookmarks.SetCount(cResult+3); m_rgBookmarks[0] = m_rgBookmarks[1] = m_rgBookmarks[2] = -1; for(int i=3;i<cResult+3;i++) { m_rgBookmarks[i] = i-2; } HRESULT hr = SetFetchSize(this); if(FAILED(hr)) return hr; if(bRegist) GetSessionPtr()->RegisterTxnCallback(this, true); return S_OK; } HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::InitFromSession(DBID *pTID, char flag) { int hConn; { // 아직 m_eType을 설정하지 않았으므로 // CCUBRIDRowset::GetSessionPtr()을 쓸 수 없다. HRESULT hr = CCUBRIDSession::GetSessionPtr(this)->GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IOpenRowset)); } /* 아직 미지원 CComVariant var; GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_ROWSET_ASYNCH, &var); ATLASSERT(V_VT(&var)==VT_I4); m_bAsynch = ( (V_I4(&var)&DBPROPVAL_ASYNCH_POPULATEONDEMAND) != 0 ); */ int hReq, cResult; { CComVariant var; GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_MAXROWS, &var); HRESULT hr = Util::OpenTable(hConn, pTID->uName.pwszName, &hReq, &cResult, flag, m_bAsynch, V_I4(&var)); if(FAILED(hr)) return hr; } m_hReq = hReq; m_eType = FromSession; m_strTableName = m_strCommandText; return InitCommon(cResult); } HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::InitFromCommand(int hReq, int cResult, bool bAsynch) { /* 아직 미지원 m_bAsynch = bAsynch; */ m_eType = FromCommand; Util::ExtractTableName(m_strCommandText, m_strTableName); return InitCommon(cResult); } /* HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::InitFromRow(int hReq, int cResult) { m_eType = FromRow; return InitCommon(hReq, cResult); } */ HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::Reexecute() { int hConn; { HRESULT hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if(FAILED(hr)) return E_FAIL; } int cResult = 0; char flag = CCI_PREPARE_INCLUDE_OID | CCI_PREPARE_UPDATABLE; { if(m_eType==FromCommand) { int &hReq = GetCommandPtr()->m_hReq; cci_close_req_handle(hReq); hReq = 0; T_CCI_ERROR err_buf; hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(m_strCommandText.m_str), flag, &err_buf); if(hReq>0) { CComVariant var; GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_MAXROWS, &var); //cci_set_max_row(hReq, V_I4(&var)); cResult = cci_execute(hReq, 0, 0, &err_buf); } else hReq = 0; } else if(m_eType==FromSession) { CComVariant var; GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_MAXROWS, &var); int hReq = 0; HRESULT hr = Util::OpenTable(hConn, m_strCommandText, &hReq, &cResult, flag, false, V_I4(&var)); if(FAILED(hr)) return E_FAIL; m_hReq = hReq; } } InitCommon(cResult, false); m_nStatus = 0; return S_OK; } void CCUBRIDRowset::TxnCallback(const ITxnCallback *pOwner) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::TxnCallback\n"); ITxnCallback *pMyOwner = this; if(m_eType==FromCommand) pMyOwner = GetCommandPtr(); if(pOwner!=pMyOwner) { cci_close_req_handle(m_hReq); m_hReq = 0; m_nStatus = 1; } else { //m_nStatus = 2; // RestartPosition시 질의를 재실행 m_nStatus = 0; // RestartPosition시 질의를 재실행하지 않음 } } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::AddRefAccessor(HACCESSOR hAccessor, DBREFCOUNT *pcRefCount) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IAccessor), "This object is in a zombie state"); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::AddRefAccessor(hAccessor, pcRefCount); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IAccessor)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::CreateAccessor(DBACCESSORFLAGS dwAccessorFlags, DBCOUNTITEM cBindings, const DBBINDING rgBindings[], DBLENGTH cbRowSize, HACCESSOR *phAccessor, DBBINDSTATUS rgStatus[]) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IAccessor), "This object is in a zombie state"); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::CreateAccessor(dwAccessorFlags, cBindings, rgBindings, cbRowSize, phAccessor, rgStatus); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IAccessor)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetBindings(HACCESSOR hAccessor, DBACCESSORFLAGS *pdwAccessorFlags, DBCOUNTITEM *pcBindings, DBBINDING **prgBindings) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IAccessor), "This object is in a zombie state"); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::GetBindings(hAccessor, pdwAccessorFlags, pcBindings, prgBindings); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IAccessor)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::ReleaseAccessor(HACCESSOR hAccessor, DBREFCOUNT *pcRefCount) { ClearError(); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::ReleaseAccessor(hAccessor, pcRefCount); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IAccessor)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetColumnDefaultValue(CCUBRIDRowset* pv) { HRESULT hr = S_OK; int hConn, hReq, res; T_CCI_ERROR error; if (!pv->m_Columns.m_defaultVal) { hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn); if (FAILED(hr)) return hr; res = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(m_strTableName.m_str), NULL, CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error); if (res<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo)); hReq = res; res = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error); if(pv->m_Columns.m_cColumns > 0 && res==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo)); if(res<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo)); pv->m_Columns.m_defaultVal = new CAtlArray<CStringA>(); while(1) { char* buffer; int ind; res = cci_fetch(hReq, &error); if(res<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo)); res = cci_get_data(hReq, 9, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &buffer, &ind); if(res<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo)); if (ind == -1) pv->m_Columns.m_defaultVal->Add(""); else { ATLASSERT(buffer); pv->m_Columns.m_defaultVal->Add(buffer); } res = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error); if(res==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break; } cci_close_req_handle(hReq); } return hr; } ATLCOLUMNINFO* CCUBRIDRowset::GetColumnInfo(CCUBRIDRowset *pv, DBORDINAL *pcCols) { if(!pv->m_Columns.m_pInfo) { CComVariant var; pv->GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_BOOKMARKS, &var); HRESULT hr = pv->m_Columns.GetColumnInfo(pv->GetRequestHandle(), V_BOOL(&var)==ATL_VARIANT_TRUE, pv->GetDataSourcePtr()->PARAM_MAX_STRING_LENGTH); if(FAILED(hr)) return NULL; //Changable일 경우만 default 값을 가져온다. //CComVariant varChange, varUpdate; //pv->GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_IRowsetChange, &varChange); //pv->GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_IRowsetUpdate, &varUpdate); //if (varChange.boolVal == ATL_VARIANT_TRUE || varUpdate.boolVal == ATL_VARIANT_TRUE) //{ // pv->GetColumnDefaultValue(pv); // //실패해도 에러 리턴 안함 //} // TODO: Command 쪽에도 추가? // 컬럼별 FINDCOMPAREOPS 등록 { ULONG iCurSet, iCurProp; pv->GetIndexofPropSet(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, &iCurSet); pv->GetIndexofPropIdinPropSet(iCurSet, DBPROP_FINDCOMPAREOPS, &iCurProp); DBPROP prop; prop.dwPropertyID = DBPROP_FINDCOMPAREOPS; prop.dwStatus = DBSTATUS_S_OK; prop.dwOptions = 0; prop.vValue.vt = VT_I4; for(int i=0;i<pv->m_Columns.m_cColumns;i++) { pv->CDBIDOps::CopyDBIDs(&prop.colid, &pv->m_Columns.m_pInfo[i].columnid); prop.vValue.lVal = ::Type::GetFindCompareOps(pv->m_Columns.m_pInfo[i].wType); pv->SetProperty(iCurSet, iCurProp, &prop); } } } if(pcCols) *pcCols = pv->m_Columns.m_cColumns; return pv->m_Columns.m_pInfo; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetColumnInfo(DBORDINAL *pcColumns, DBCOLUMNINFO **prgInfo, OLECHAR **ppStringsBuffer) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo), "This object is in a zombie state"); HRESULT hr = IColumnsInfoImpl<CCUBRIDRowset>::GetColumnInfo(pcColumns, prgInfo, ppStringsBuffer); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo)); return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::MapColumnIDs(DBORDINAL cColumnIDs, const DBID rgColumnIDs[], DBORDINAL rgColumns[]) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo), "This object is in a zombie state"); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::MapColumnIDs(cColumnIDs, rgColumnIDs, rgColumns); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::CanConvert(DBTYPE wFromType, DBTYPE wToType, DBCONVERTFLAGS dwConvertFlags) { ClearError(); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::CanConvert(wFromType, wToType, dwConvertFlags); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IConvertType)); else return hr; } // MapClass의 key와 RowClass의 초기화(ReadData 호출) 때문에 override HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::CreateRow(DBROWOFFSET lRowsOffset, DBCOUNTITEM &cRowsObtained, HROW *rgRows) { CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow = NULL; ATLASSERT(lRowsOffset >= 0); CCUBRIDRowsetRow::KeyType key = lRowsOffset+1; ATLASSERT(key > 0); bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup(key,pRow); if (!bFound || pRow == NULL) { DBORDINAL cCols; ATLCOLUMNINFO *pInfo = GetColumnInfo(this, &cCols); ATLTRY(pRow = new CCUBRIDRowsetRow(lRowsOffset, cCols, pInfo, m_spConvert, m_Columns.m_defaultVal)) if (pRow == NULL) return E_OUTOFMEMORY; bool bSensitive = false; { CComVariant var; GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_OWNUPDATEDELETE, &var); bSensitive = (V_BOOL(&var)==VARIANT_TRUE); } HRESULT hr = pRow->ReadData(GetRequestHandle(), false, bSensitive); if(FAILED(hr)) { delete pRow; pRow = NULL; return hr; } _ATLTRY { m_rgRowHandles.SetAt(key, pRow); } _ATLCATCH( e ) { _ATLDELETEEXCEPTION( e ); delete pRow; pRow = NULL; return E_OUTOFMEMORY; } } else // found pRow { if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_INVALIDROW) return DB_E_DELETEDROW; } pRow->AddRefRow(); m_bReset = false; rgRows[cRowsObtained++] = (HROW)key; return S_OK; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::AddRefRows(DBCOUNTITEM cRows, const HROW rghRows[], DBREFCOUNT rgRefCounts[], DBROWSTATUS rgRowStatus[]) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "This object is in a zombie state"); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::AddRefRows(cRows, rghRows, rgRefCounts, rgRowStatus); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetData(HROW hRow, HACCESSOR hAccessor, void *pDstData) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "This object is in a zombie state"); ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, _T("IRowset::GetData\n")); HRESULT hr; CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow = 0; ATLBINDINGS *pBinding = 0; { // check arguments and prepare data if(hRow==NULL || !m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow) || pRow==NULL) return RaiseError(DB_E_BADROWHANDLE, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); if(!m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding) || pBinding==NULL) return RaiseError(DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); if(pDstData==NULL && pBinding->cBindings!=0) return RaiseError(E_INVALIDARG, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); } if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_INVALIDROW || pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_DELETED) return RaiseError(DB_E_DELETEDROW, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); DBROWCOUNT dwBookmark = pRow->m_iRowset+3;//Util::FindBookmark(m_rgBookmarks, (LONG)pRow->m_iRowset+1); hr = pRow->WriteData(pBinding, pDstData, dwBookmark, this); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); else return hr; } HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::GetNextRowsAsynch(HCHAPTER hReserved, DBROWOFFSET lRowsOffset, DBROWCOUNT cRows, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsObtained, HROW **prghRows) { // TODO: backward fetch 미테스트(아마 잘 안 될듯) // bookmark 미구현 ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetNextRowsAsynch\n"); if(prghRows==NULL || pcRowsObtained==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; if(cRows==0) return S_OK; if(lRowsOffset<0 && !m_bCanScrollBack) return DB_E_CANTSCROLLBACKWARDS; if(cRows<0 && !m_bCanFetchBack) return DB_E_CANTFETCHBACKWARDS; // In the case where the user is moving backwards after moving forwards, // we do not wrap around to the end of the rowset. if(m_iRowset==0 && !m_bReset && cRows<0) return DB_S_ENDOFROWSET; if(lRowsOffset<0 && m_bReset) return DB_E_CANTSCROLLBACKWARDS; // 아직 데이터가 다 없는데 backward가 가능한가? int iStepSize = ( cRows >= 0 ? 1 : -1 ); cRows = AbsVal(cRows); // if cRows==MINLONG_PTR? DBROWOFFSET lTmpRows = lRowsOffset; lRowsOffset += m_iRowset; CComHeapPtr<HROW> rghRowsAllocated; if(*prghRows==NULL) { rghRowsAllocated.Allocate(cRows); // 일단 최대로 잡는다. if(rghRowsAllocated==NULL) return E_OUTOFMEMORY; *prghRows = rghRowsAllocated; } HRESULT hr = S_OK; while(lRowsOffset>=0 && cRows!=0) { // cRows > cRowsInSet && iStepSize < 0 if (lRowsOffset == 0 && cRows > 0 && iStepSize < 0) break; hr = CreateRow(lRowsOffset, *pcRowsObtained, *prghRows); if(FAILED(hr)) { RefRows(*pcRowsObtained, *prghRows, NULL, NULL, FALSE); for(ULONG iRowDel=0;iRowDel<*pcRowsObtained;iRowDel++) (*prghRows)[iRowDel] = NULL; *pcRowsObtained = 0; return hr; } // TODO: hr==DB_S_ENDOFROWSET이면 다 읽었다는 표시인데 // m_bAsynch=false로 바꾸는게 좋을까? // 이 경우 Commit에 의해 다시 테이블을 읽어들일때 // 문제가 될지도 모르겠다. if(hr!=S_OK) break; if(m_rgRowData.GetCount()<=(size_t)lRowsOffset) m_rgRowData.SetCount(lRowsOffset+1); if(m_rgBookmarks.GetCount()<=(size_t)lRowsOffset+3) m_rgBookmarks.SetCount(lRowsOffset+4); m_rgBookmarks[lRowsOffset+3] = lRowsOffset+1; cRows--; lRowsOffset += iStepSize; } m_iRowset = lRowsOffset; if(SUCCEEDED(hr) && *pcRowsObtained>0) rghRowsAllocated.Detach(); else { if(rghRowsAllocated) *prghRows = 0; // 입력시 *prghRows==NULL이고 에러가 발생했으면 다시 NULL로 만든다. } return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetNextRows(HCHAPTER hReserved, DBROWOFFSET lRowsOffset, DBROWCOUNT cRows, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsObtained, HROW **prghRows) { ClearError(); if(pcRowsObtained) *pcRowsObtained = 0; if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "This object is in a zombie state"); if(cRows==0) return S_OK; CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowset)); if(!m_bExternalFetch) CHECK_CANHOLDROWS(__uuidof(IRowset)); if(m_bAsynch) return GetNextRowsAsynch(hReserved, lRowsOffset, cRows, pcRowsObtained, prghRows); bool bProvAlloc = (pcRowsObtained && prghRows && *prghRows==0); HRESULT hr; hr = _RowsetBaseClass::GetNextRows(hReserved, lRowsOffset, cRows, pcRowsObtained, prghRows); if(bProvAlloc && *pcRowsObtained==0) { // ATL Provider Templates의 버그 *prghRows = 0; } if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::ReleaseRows(DBCOUNTITEM cRows, const HROW rghRows[], DBROWOPTIONS rgRowOptions[], DBREFCOUNT rgRefCounts[], DBROWSTATUS rgRowStatus[]) { ClearError(); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::ReleaseRows(cRows, rghRows, rgRowOptions, rgRefCounts, rgRowStatus); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::RestartPosition(HCHAPTER hReserved) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "This object is in a zombie state"); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::RestartPosition(hReserved); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); cci_fetch_buffer_clear(GetRequestHandle()); if(m_nStatus==2) { hr = Reexecute(); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "Failed to reexecute the command"); return DB_S_COMMANDREEXECUTED; } return S_OK; } // Provider Templates의 구현은 DELETED 상태인 ROW에 대해 DB_E_DELETEDROW를 반환한다. // spec은 INVALIDROW에 대해서 반환하게 되어 있다. STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::IsSameRow(HROW hThisRow, HROW hThatRow) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetIdentity), "This object is in a zombie state"); ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::IsSameRow\n"); // Validate row handles CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow1; if( ! m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((CCUBRIDRowsetRow::KeyType)hThisRow, pRow1) ) return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE; CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow2; if( ! m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((CCUBRIDRowsetRow::KeyType)hThatRow, pRow2) ) return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE; if (pRow1->m_status == DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW || pRow2->m_status == DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW) return DB_E_NEWLYINSERTED; if (pRow1->m_status == DBPENDINGSTATUS_INVALIDROW || pRow2->m_status == DBPENDINGSTATUS_INVALIDROW) return DB_E_DELETEDROW; return pRow1->Compare(pRow2); } HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::OnPropertyChanged(ULONG iCurSet, DBPROP* pDBProp) { HRESULT hr = CUBRIDOnPropertyChanged(this, iCurSet, pDBProp); if(hr==S_FALSE) return _RowsetBaseClass::OnPropertyChanged(iCurSet, pDBProp); else return hr; } HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::IsValidValue(ULONG iCurSet, DBPROP* pDBProp) { ATLASSERT(pDBProp); if(pDBProp->dwPropertyID==DBPROP_ROWSET_ASYNCH) { // TODO: PREPOPULATE와 POPULATEONDEMAND 둘 다 세팅하는 건 에러겠지? LONG val = V_I4(&pDBProp->vValue); if(val==0 || val==DBPROPVAL_ASYNCH_PREPOPULATE // --> synchronous || val==DBPROPVAL_ASYNCH_POPULATEONDEMAND) // --> asynchronous return S_OK; return S_FALSE; } return _RowsetBaseClass::IsValidValue(iCurSet, pDBProp); } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetProperties(const ULONG cPropertyIDSets, const DBPROPIDSET rgPropertyIDSets[], ULONG *pcPropertySets, DBPROPSET **prgPropertySets) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetInfo), "This object is in a zombie state"); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetInfo)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetSpecification(REFIID riid, IUnknown **ppSpecification) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetInfo), "This object is in a zombie state"); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::GetSpecification(riid, ppSpecification); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetInfo)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetRowFromHROW(IUnknown *pUnkOuter, HROW hRow, REFIID riid, IUnknown **ppUnk) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IGetRow), "This object is in a zombie state"); ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetRowFromHROW\n"); DBCOUNTITEM iRowset; { // check arguments CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow = 0; CComPtr<IUnknown> spUnk; hr = pRow->QueryInterface(&spUnk); if(FAILED(hr)) { delete pRow; // 참조되지 않았기 때문에 수동으로 지운다. return hr; } // Rowset object의 IUnknown을 Row의 Site로 설정한다. ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetURLFromHROW\n"); return RaiseError(DB_E_NOTSUPPORTED, 0, __uuidof(IGetRow)); } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::FindNextRow(HCHAPTER hChapter, HACCESSOR hAccessor, void *pFindValue, DBCOMPAREOP CompareOp, DBBKMARK cbBookmark, const BYTE *pBookmark, DBROWOFFSET lRowsOffset, DBROWCOUNT cRows, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsObtained, HROW **prghRows) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::FindNextRow\n"); ClearError(); if(pcRowsObtained) *pcRowsObtained = 0; if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetFind), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetFind)); if(pcRowsObtained==NULL || prghRows==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; if(cbBookmark!=0 && pBookmark==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; if(hChapter!=DB_NULL_HCHAPTER) return DB_E_BADCHAPTER; CHECK_CANHOLDROWS(__uuidof(IRowsetFind)); // 바인딩 정보를 구함 ATLBINDINGS *pBinding; { // 스펙에 DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE, DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE, E_INVALIDARG를 // 반환하는 경우는 정의되어 있지 않지만 해주는게 맞는 것 같다. bool bFound = m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding); if(!bFound || pBinding==NULL) return DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE; if(!(pBinding->dwAccessorFlags & DBACCESSOR_ROWDATA)) return DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE; // row accessor 가 아니다. if(pBinding->cBindings!=1) return DB_E_BADBINDINFO; } // 나중에 체크하지만 LTM을 위해 중복 { DBCOMPAREOP LocalOp = CompareOp & ~DBCOMPAREOPS_CASESENSITIVE & ~DBCOMPAREOPS_CASEINSENSITIVE; if(LocalOp<0 || LocalOp>DBCOMPAREOPS_NOTCONTAINS) return DB_E_BADCOMPAREOP; if((CompareOp & DBCOMPAREOPS_CASESENSITIVE) && (CompareOp & DBCOMPAREOPS_CASEINSENSITIVE)) return DB_E_BADCOMPAREOP; } if(cRows==0 && cbBookmark!=0) return S_OK; DBROWOFFSET iDir = 1; if(cRows<0) { iDir = -1; cRows = -cRows; } if(cRows==0) { iDir = (m_bFindForward?1:-1); } m_bFindForward = (iDir==1); CComHeapPtr<HROW> rghRowsAllocated; if(*prghRows==NULL) { rghRowsAllocated.Allocate(cRows?cRows:1); if(rghRowsAllocated==NULL) return E_OUTOFMEMORY; *prghRows = rghRowsAllocated; } DBROWOFFSET iRowsetTemp = -1; if(cbBookmark!=0) { if(!m_bCanScrollBack) return DB_E_CANTSCROLLBACKWARDS; HRESULT hr = ValidateBookmark(cbBookmark, pBookmark); if(FAILED(hr)) return hr; iRowsetTemp = m_iRowset; // cache the current rowset // 시작 점을 찾는다. if(cbBookmark==1) { if(*pBookmark==DBBMK_FIRST) m_iRowset = 1; else // *pBookmark==DBBMK_LAST m_iRowset = (DBCOUNTITEM)m_rgRowData.GetCount(); } else { m_iRowset = m_rgBookmarks[*pBookmark]; } if(iDir==1) m_iRowset--; } while(1) { DBCOUNTITEM cTmp; HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[0]; m_bExternalFetch = true; HRESULT hr = GetNextRows(hChapter, lRowsOffset, iDir, &cTmp, &phRow); m_bExternalFetch = false; lRowsOffset = 0; // 첫 fetch 때만 lRowsOffset을 적용 if(FAILED(hr) || hr==DB_S_ENDOFROWSET) goto error; // 조건 검사 bool bMatch = true; if(CompareOp!=DBCOMPAREOPS_IGNORE) { CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)*phRow, pRow); ATLASSERT(bFound && pRow!=NULL); } DBBINDING &rBinding = pBinding->pBindings[0]; hr = pRow->Compare(pFindValue, CompareOp, rBinding); if(hr==S_FALSE) bMatch = false; else if(hr!=S_OK) goto error; } if(bMatch) { (*pcRowsObtained)++; break; } else ReleaseRows(1, phRow, NULL, NULL, NULL); continue; error: if(rghRowsAllocated) // 메모리 해제는 자동적으로 이루어진다. *prghRows = 0; if(iRowsetTemp!=-1) m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp; return hr; } if(cRows>1) { // fetch last rows DBCOUNTITEM cTmp; HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[1]; m_bExternalFetch = true; GetNextRows(hChapter, 0, (cRows-1)*iDir, &cTmp, &phRow); // TODO: return value 검사? m_bExternalFetch = false; *pcRowsObtained += cTmp; } else if(cRows==0) { // handle은 반환하지 않고 fetch position만 변경되는 효과를 낸다. HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[0]; ReleaseRows(1, phRow, NULL, NULL, NULL); *pcRowsObtained = 0; if(rghRowsAllocated) // 메모리 해제는 자동적으로 이루어진다. *prghRows = 0; } // bookmark에서 찾기 시작한 경우에는 fetch position을 복구한다. if(iRowsetTemp!=-1) m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp; // prghRows!=NULL이였으면 rghRowsAllocated==NULL // prghRows==NULL이였으면 이미 prghRows==rghRowsAllocated // 따라서 소유권만 없애면 된다. rghRowsAllocated.Detach(); return ( cRows==*pcRowsObtained ? S_OK : DB_S_ENDOFROWSET ); } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData(HCHAPTER hChapter, DBCOUNTITEM cRows, const HROW rghRows[], BOOL fOverWrite, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsRefreshed, HROW **prghRowsRefreshed, DBROWSTATUS **prgRowStatus) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData\n"); ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh)); if(pcRowsRefreshed) *pcRowsRefreshed = 0; if(prghRowsRefreshed) *prghRowsRefreshed = 0; if(prgRowStatus) *prgRowStatus = 0; if(cRows!=0 && rghRows==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; if(pcRowsRefreshed!=NULL && prghRowsRefreshed==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; DBCOUNTITEM cRowsLocal = ( cRows==0 ? (DBCOUNTITEM)m_rgRowHandles.GetCount() : cRows ); if(cRowsLocal==0) return S_OK; // pcRowsRefreshed!=NULL 이면 HROW와 DBROWSTATUS를 반환한다. // 이 이후로는 메모리를 해제할 일 없음 if(pcRowsRefreshed) { *prghRowsRefreshed = (HROW *)CoTaskMemAlloc(cRowsLocal * sizeof(HROW)); if(*prghRowsRefreshed==0) { return E_OUTOFMEMORY; } if(prgRowStatus) { *prgRowStatus = (DBROWSTATUS *)CoTaskMemAlloc(cRowsLocal * sizeof(DBROWSTATUS)); if(*prgRowStatus==0) { CoTaskMemFree(*prghRowsRefreshed); *prghRowsRefreshed = 0; return E_OUTOFMEMORY; } } *pcRowsRefreshed = cRowsLocal; } DBROWSTATUS statTmp; bool bSucceeded = false, bFailed = false; POSITION pos = m_rgRowHandles.GetStartPosition(); for(DBCOUNTITEM i=0;i<cRowsLocal;i++) { ATLASSERT(pos!=NULL); HROW hRow = ( cRows==0 ? m_rgRowHandles.GetNextKey(pos) : rghRows[i] ); if(pcRowsRefreshed) (*prghRowsRefreshed)[i] = hRow; DBROWSTATUS &rCurStat = ( (pcRowsRefreshed&&prgRowStatus) ? (*prgRowStatus)[i] : statTmp ); CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow); if(!bFound || pRow==NULL) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_INVALID; bFailed = true; continue; } } if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_PENDINGINSERT; bFailed = true; continue; } if(!fOverWrite && (pRow->m_status==0 || pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_UNCHANGED)) { // TODO: 반환값이 정확한 건지 스펙을 보고는 잘 모르겠다. rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_S_OK; bSucceeded = true; continue; } HRESULT hr = pRow->ReadData(GetRequestHandle(), false, true); if(hr==DB_E_DELETEDROW) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_DELETED; bFailed = true; continue; } rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_S_OK; bSucceeded = true; } if(!bFailed) return S_OK; else return bSucceeded ? DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED : DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData(HROW hRow, HACCESSOR hAccessor, void *pData) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData\n"); ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh)); // 바인딩 정보를 구함 ATLBINDINGS *pBinding; { bool bFound = m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding); if(!bFound || pBinding==NULL) return DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE; if(!(pBinding->dwAccessorFlags & DBACCESSOR_ROWDATA)) return DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE; // row accessor 가 아니다. if(pData==NULL && pBinding->cBindings!=0) return E_INVALIDARG; } // Attempt to locate the row in our map CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow); if(!bFound || pRow==NULL) return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE; } if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW) return DB_E_PENDINGINSERT; DBORDINAL cCols; ATLCOLUMNINFO *pInfo = GetColumnInfo(this, &cCols); DBROWCOUNT dwBookmark = pRow->m_iRowset+3;//Util::FindBookmark(m_rgBookmarks, (LONG)pRow->m_iRowset+1); // 임시 RowClass를 통해 storage에서 데이터를 읽어온 후, pData로 전송한다. } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::Compare(HCHAPTER hReserved, DBBKMARK cbBookmark1, const BYTE *pBookmark1, DBBKMARK cbBookmark2, const BYTE *pBookmark2, DBCOMPARE *pComparison) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetLocate), "This object is in a zombie state"); 72  return static_cast<CCUBRIDRowset *>((IRowset *)spCom);
73 }

80 int CCUBRIDRowset::GetRequestHandle()
81 {
82  switch(m_eType)
83  {
84  case FromSession:
85  return m_hReq;
86  case FromCommand:
87  return GetCommandPtr()->m_hReq;
88  case FromRow:
89  return 0; // TODO
90  default: // Invalid
91  return 0;
92  }
93 }

97 {
98  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "CCUBRIDRowset::CCUBRIDRowset\n");

103 CCUBRIDRowset::~CCUBRIDRowset()
104 {
105  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 3, "CCUBRIDRowset::~CCUBRIDRowset\n");
106 
107  CCUBRIDSession *pSession = GetSessionPtr();
108  if(pSession)
109  {
110  //pSession->RowsetCommit();
111 #if 1
112  if(m_bIsChangeable) pSession->RowsetCommit();
113 #endif
114  pSession->RegisterTxnCallback(this, false);
115  }
116 }

118 HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::ValidateCommandID(DBID *pTableID, DBID *pIndexID)
119 {
120  HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::ValidateCommandID(pTableID, pIndexID);
121  if (hr != S_OK)
122  return hr;
123 
124  if(pIndexID)
125  return RaiseError(DB_E_NOINDEX, 0, __uuidof(IOpenRowset)); // 인덱스를 지원하지 않는다.
126 
127  if(pTableID && (pTableID->uName.pwszName==NULL || wcslen(pTableID->uName.pwszName)==0))
128  return RaiseError(DB_E_NOTABLE, 0, __uuidof(IOpenRowset)); // 테이블 이름이 없다.
129 
130  return S_OK;
131 }
132 
133 // cci_fetch_size를 설정한다.
134 static HRESULT SetFetchSize(CCUBRIDRowset *pRowset)
135 {
136  CCUBRIDDataSource *pDS = pRowset->GetDataSourcePtr();
137  CComVariant var;
138  pDS->GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_UNIPROVIDER_DBINIT, DBPROP_UNIPROVIDER_FETCH_SIZE, &var);
139 
140  int rc = cci_fetch_size(pRowset->GetRequestHandle(), V_I4(&var));
141  if(rc<0)
142  RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "Failed to set the fetch size");
143  return S_OK;
144 }

146 HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::InitCommon(int cResult, bool bRegist)
147 {
148  m_rgRowData.SetCount(cResult);
149 
150  // 1과 2는 DBBMK_FIRST, DBBMK_LAST를 위해 비워놓는다.
151  // cbBookmark가 1과 4로 다르긴 한데
152  // IRowsetLocateImpl은 구현이 잘못되서 구별을 잘 못한다.
153  m_rgBookmarks.SetCount(cResult+3);
154  m_rgBookmarks[0] = m_rgBookmarks[1] = m_rgBookmarks[2] = -1;
155  for(int i=3;i<cResult+3;i++)
156  {
157  m_rgBookmarks[i] = i-2;
158  }
159 
160  HRESULT hr = SetFetchSize(this);
161  if(FAILED(hr)) return hr;
162 
163  if(bRegist)
164  GetSessionPtr()->RegisterTxnCallback(this, true);
165 
166  return S_OK;
167 }
168

} if(cRows==0 && cbBookmark!=0) return S_OK; DBROWOFFSET iDir = 1; if(cRows<0) { iDir = -1; cRows = -cRows; } if(cRows==0) { iDir = (m_bFindForward?1:-1); } m_bFindForward = (iDir==1); CComHeapPtr<HROW> rghRowsAllocated; } return S_OK; } // Provider Templates의 구현은 DELETED 상태인 ROW에 대해 DB_E_DELETEDROW를 반환한다. // spec은 INVALIDROW에 대해서 반환하게 되어 있다. } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetProperties(const ULONG cPropertyIDSets, const DBPROPIDSET rgPropertyIDSets[], ULONG *pcPropertySets, DBPROPSET **prgPropertySets) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetInfo), "This object is in a zombie state"); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::GetSpecification(riid, ppSpecification); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetInfo)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetRowFromHROW(IUnknown *pUnkOuter, HROW hRow, REFIID riid, IUnknown **ppUnk) { ClearError(); ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetURLFromHROW\n"); return RaiseError(DB_E_NOTSUPPORTED, 0, __uuidof(IGetRow)); } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::FindNextRow(HCHAPTER hChapter, HACCESSOR hAccessor, void *pFindValue, DBCOMPAREOP CompareOp, DBBKMARK cbBookmark, const BYTE *pBookmark, DBROWOFFSET lRowsOffset, DBROWCOUNT cRows, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsObtained, HROW **prghRows) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::FindNextRow\n"); ClearError(); if(pcRowsObtained) *pcRowsObtained = 0; if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetFind), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetFind)); // 바인딩 정보를 구함 ATLBINDINGS *pBinding; { // 스펙에 DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE, DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE, E_INVALIDARG를 // 반환하는 경우는 정의되어 있지 않지만 해주는게 맞는 것 같다. bool bFound = m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding); } if(cRows==0 && cbBookmark!=0) return S_OK; DBROWOFFSET iDir = 1; if(cRows<0) { iDir = -1; cRows = -cRows; } if(cRows==0) { iDir = (m_bFindForward?1:-1); } m_bFindForward = (iDir==1); CComHeapPtr<HROW> rghRowsAllocated; if(*prghRows==NULL) { rghRowsAllocated.Allocate(cRows?cRows:1); if(rghRowsAllocated==NULL) return E_OUTOFMEMORY; *prghRows = rghRowsAllocated; } DBROWOFFSET iRowsetTemp = -1; if(cbBookmark!=0) { if(!m_bCanScrollBack) return DB_E_CANTSCROLLBACKWARDS; // 조건 검사 bool bMatch = true; if(CompareOp!=DBCOMPAREOPS_IGNORE) { CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)*phRow, pRow); ATLASSERT(bFound && pRow!=NULL); } DBBINDING &rBinding = pBinding->pBindings[0]; hr = pRow->Compare(pFindValue, CompareOp, rBinding); if(hr==S_FALSE) bMatch = false; else if(hr!=S_OK) goto error; } if(bMatch) { (*pcRowsObtained)++; break; } else ReleaseRows(1, phRow, NULL, NULL, NULL); continue; error: if(rghRowsAllocated) // 메모리 해제는 자동적으로 이루어진다. *prghRows = 0; if(iRowsetTemp!=-1) m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp; return hr; } if(cRows>1) { // fetch last rows DBCOUNTITEM cTmp; HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[1]; m_bExternalFetch = true; GetNextRows(hChapter, 0, (cRows-1)*iDir, &cTmp, &phRow); // TODO: return value 검사? m_bExternalFetch = false; *pcRowsObtained += cTmp; } else if(cRows==0) { // handle은 반환하지 않고 fetch position만 변경되는 효과를 낸다. HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[0]; ReleaseRows(1, phRow, NULL, NULL, NULL); *pcRowsObtained = 0; if(rghRowsAllocated) // 메모리 해제는 자동적으로 이루어진다. *prghRows = 0; } // bookmark에서 찾기 시작한 경우에는 fetch position을 복구한다. if(iRowsetTemp!=-1) m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp; // prghRows!=NULL이였으면 rghRowsAllocated==NULL // prghRows==NULL이였으면 이미 prghRows==rghRowsAllocated // 따라서 소유권만 없애면 된다. rghRowsAllocated.Detach(); return ( cRows==*pcRowsObtained ? S_OK : DB_S_ENDOFROWSET ); } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData(HCHAPTER hChapter, DBCOUNTITEM cRows, const HROW rghRows[], BOOL fOverWrite, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsRefreshed, HROW **prghRowsRefreshed, DBROWSTATUS **prgRowStatus) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData\n"); ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh)); if(pcRowsRefreshed) *pcRowsRefreshed = 0; if(prghRowsRefreshed) *prghRowsRefreshed = 0; if(prgRowStatus) *prgRowStatus = 0; if(cRows!=0 && rghRows==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; if(pcRowsRefreshed!=NULL && prghRowsRefreshed==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; DBCOUNTITEM cRowsLocal = ( cRows==0 ? DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED : DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData(HROW hRow, HACCESSOR hAccessor, void *pData) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData\n"); ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh)); // 바인딩 정보를 구함 ATLBINDINGS *pBinding; { bool bFound = m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding); if(!bFound || pBinding==NULL) return DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE; if(!(pBinding->dwAccessorFlags & DBACCESSOR_ROWDATA)) return DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE; // row accessor 가 아니다. if(pData==NULL && pBinding->cBindings!=0) return E_INVALIDARG; } // Attempt to locate the row in our map CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow); if(!bFound || pRow==NULL) return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE; } if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW) return DB_E_PENDINGINSERT; DBORDINAL cCols; ATLCOLUMNINFO *pInfo = GetColumnInfo(this, &cCols); DBROWCOUNT dwBookmark = pRow->m_iRowset+3;//Util::FindBookmark(m_rgBookmarks, (LONG)pRow->m_iRowset+1); // 임시 RowClass를 통해 storage에서 데이터를 읽어온 후, pData로 전송한다. 213 HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::InitFromRow(int hReq, int cResult)

219 
220 HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::Reexecute()
221 {
222  int hConn;
223  {
224  HRESULT hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn);
225  if(FAILED(hr)) return E_FAIL;
226  }
227 
228  int cResult = 0;
229  char flag = CCI_PREPARE_INCLUDE_OID | CCI_PREPARE_UPDATABLE;
230  {
231  if(m_eType==FromCommand)
232  {
233  int &hReq = GetCommandPtr()->m_hReq;
234  cci_close_req_handle(hReq);
235  hReq = 0;
236 
237  T_CCI_ERROR err_buf;
238  hReq = cci_prepare(hConn, CW2A(m_strCommandText.m_str), flag, &err_buf);
239  if(hReq>0)
240  {
241  CComVariant var;
242  GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_MAXROWS, &var);
243  //cci_set_max_row(hReq, V_I4(&var));
244 
245  cResult = cci_execute(hReq, 0, 0, &err_buf);
246  }
247  else
248  hReq = 0;
249  }
250  else if(m_eType==FromSession)
251  {
252  CComVariant var;
253  GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_MAXROWS, &var);
254 
255  int hReq = 0;
256  HRESULT hr = Util::OpenTable(hConn, m_strCommandText, &hReq, &cResult, flag, false, V_I4(&var));
257  if(FAILED(hr)) return E_FAIL;
258 
259  m_hReq = hReq;
260  }
261  }
262 
263  InitCommon(cResult, false);
264 
265  m_nStatus = 0;
266 
267  return S_OK;
268 }
269 
270 void CCUBRIDRowset::TxnCallback(const ITxnCallback *pOwner)
271 {
272  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::TxnCallback\n");
273 
274  ITxnCallback *pMyOwner = this;
275  if(m_eType==FromCommand)
276  pMyOwner = GetCommandPtr();
277 
278  if(pOwner!=pMyOwner)
279  {
280  cci_close_req_handle(m_hReq);
281  m_hReq = 0;
282  m_nStatus = 1;
283  }
284  else

continue; error: if(rghRowsAllocated) // 메모리 해제는 자동적으로 이루어진다. *prghRows = 0; if(iRowsetTemp!=-1) m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp; return hr; } if(cRows>1) { // fetch last rows DBCOUNTITEM cTmp; HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[1]; m_bExternalFetch = true; GetNextRows(hChapter, 0, (cRows-1)*iDir, &cTmp, &phRow); // TODO: return value 검사? m_bExternalFetch = false; *pcRowsObtained += cTmp; } else if(cRows==0) { // handle은 반환하지 않고 fetch position만 변경되는 효과를 낸다. S_OK : DB_S_ENDOFROWSET ); } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData(HCHAPTER hChapter, DBCOUNTITEM cRows, const HROW rghRows[], BOOL fOverWrite, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsRefreshed, HROW **prghRowsRefreshed, DBROWSTATUS **prgRowStatus) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData\n"); ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh)); if(pcRowsRefreshed) *pcRowsRefreshed = 0; if(prghRowsRefreshed) *prghRowsRefreshed = 0; if(prgRowStatus) *prgRowStatus = 0; if(cRows!=0 && rghRows==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; if(pcRowsRefreshed!=NULL && prghRowsRefreshed==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; DBCOUNTITEM cRowsLocal = ( cRows==0 ? (*prgRowStatus)[i] : statTmp ); CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow); if(!bFound || pRow==NULL) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_INVALID; bFailed = true; continue; } } if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_PENDINGINSERT; bFailed = true; continue; } if(!fOverWrite && (pRow->m_status==0 || pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_UNCHANGED)) { // TODO: 반환값이 정확한 건지 스펙을 보고는 잘 모르겠다. rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_S_OK; bSucceeded = true; continue; } HRESULT hr = pRow->ReadData(GetRequestHandle(), false, true); if(hr==DB_E_DELETEDROW) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_DELETED; bFailed = true; continue; } rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_S_OK; bSucceeded = true; } if(!bFailed) return S_OK; else return bSucceeded ? DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED : DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData(HROW hRow, HACCESSOR hAccessor, void *pData) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData\n"); ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh)); // 바인딩 정보를 구함 ATLBINDINGS *pBinding; { bool bFound = m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding); if(!bFound || pBinding==NULL) return DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE; if(!(pBinding->dwAccessorFlags & DBACCESSOR_ROWDATA)) return DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE; // row accessor 가 아니다. if(pData==NULL && pBinding->cBindings!=0) return E_INVALIDARG; } // Attempt to locate the row in our map CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow); if(!bFound || pRow==NULL) return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE; } if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW) return DB_E_PENDINGINSERT; DBORDINAL cCols; ATLCOLUMNINFO *pInfo = GetColumnInfo(this, &cCols); DBROWCOUNT dwBookmark = pRow->m_iRowset+3;//Util::FindBookmark(m_rgBookmarks, (LONG)pRow->m_iRowset+1); // 임시 RowClass를 통해 storage에서 데이터를 읽어온 후, pData로 전송한다. 339 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetColumnDefaultValue(CCUBRIDRowset* pv)
340 {
341  HRESULT hr = S_OK;
342  int hConn, hReq, res;
343  T_CCI_ERROR error;
344 
345  if (!pv->m_Columns.m_defaultVal)
346  {
347  hr = GetConnectionHandle(&hConn);
348  if (FAILED(hr)) return hr;
349 
350  res = cci_schema_info(hConn, CCI_SCH_ATTRIBUTE, CW2A(m_strTableName.m_str), NULL,
351  CCI_ATTR_NAME_PATTERN_MATCH, &error);
352  if (res<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo));
353  hReq = res;
354 
355  res = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_FIRST, &error);
356  if(pv->m_Columns.m_cColumns > 0 && res==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA)
357  return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo));
358 
359  if(res<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo));
360 
361  pv->m_Columns.m_defaultVal = new CAtlArray<CStringA>();
362 
363  while(1)
364  {
365  char* buffer;
366  int ind;
367 
368  res = cci_fetch(hReq, &error);
369  if(res<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo));
370 
371  res = cci_get_data(hReq, 9, CCI_A_TYPE_STR, &buffer, &ind);
372  if(res<0) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 0, __uuidof(IColumnsInfo));
373 
374  if (ind == -1)
375  pv->m_Columns.m_defaultVal->Add("");
376  else
377  {
378  ATLASSERT(buffer);
379  pv->m_Columns.m_defaultVal->Add(buffer);
380  }
381  res = cci_cursor(hReq, 1, CCI_CURSOR_CURRENT, &error);
382  if(res==CCI_ER_NO_MORE_DATA) break;
383  }
384 
385  cci_close_req_handle(hReq);
386  }
387 
388  return hr;
389 }

} STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetNextRows(HCHAPTER hReserved, DBROWOFFSET lRowsOffset, DBROWCOUNT cRows, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsObtained, HROW **prghRows) { ClearError(); if(pcRowsObtained) *pcRowsObtained = 0; S_OK : DB_S_ENDOFROWSET ); } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData(HCHAPTER hChapter, DBCOUNTITEM cRows, const HROW rghRows[], BOOL fOverWrite, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsRefreshed, HROW **prghRowsRefreshed, DBROWSTATUS **prgRowStatus) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData\n"); ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh)); if(pcRowsRefreshed) *pcRowsRefreshed = 0; if(prghRowsRefreshed) *prghRowsRefreshed = 0; if(prgRowStatus) *prgRowStatus = 0; if(cRows!=0 && rghRows==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; if(pcRowsRefreshed!=NULL && prghRowsRefreshed==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; DBCOUNTITEM cRowsLocal = ( cRows==0 ? (*prgRowStatus)[i] : statTmp ); CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow); if(!bFound || pRow==NULL) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_INVALID; bFailed = true; continue; } } if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_PENDINGINSERT; bFailed = true; continue; } if(!fOverWrite && (pRow->m_status==0 || pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_UNCHANGED)) { // TODO: 반환값이 정확한 건지 스펙을 보고는 잘 모르겠다. rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_S_OK; bSucceeded = true; continue; } HRESULT hr = pRow->ReadData(GetRequestHandle(), false, true); if(hr==DB_E_DELETEDROW) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_DELETED; bFailed = true; continue; } rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_S_OK; bSucceeded = true; } if(!bFailed) return S_OK; else return bSucceeded ? DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED : DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData(HROW hRow, HACCESSOR hAccessor, void *pData) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData\n"); ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh)); // 바인딩 정보를 구함 ATLBINDINGS *pBinding; { bool bFound = m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding); if(!bFound || pBinding==NULL) return DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE; if(!(pBinding->dwAccessorFlags & DBACCESSOR_ROWDATA)) return DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE; // row accessor 가 아니다. if(pData==NULL && pBinding->cBindings!=0) return E_INVALIDARG; } // Attempt to locate the row in our map CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow); if(!bFound || pRow==NULL) return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE; } if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW) return DB_E_PENDINGINSERT; DBORDINAL cCols; ATLCOLUMNINFO *pInfo = GetColumnInfo(this, &cCols); DBROWCOUNT dwBookmark = pRow->m_iRowset+3;//Util::FindBookmark(m_rgBookmarks, (LONG)pRow->m_iRowset+1); // 임시 RowClass를 통해 storage에서 데이터를 읽어온 후, pData로 전송한다. CCUBRIDRowsetRow OrigRow(pRow->m_iRowset, cCols, pInfo, m_spConvert, m_Columns.m_defaultVal); OrigRow.ReadData(GetRequestHandle(), false, true); return OrigRow.WriteData(pBinding, pData, dwBookmark); } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::Compare(HCHAPTER hReserved, DBBKMARK cbBookmark1, const BYTE *pBookmark1, DBBKMARK cbBookmark2, const BYTE *pBookmark2, DBCOMPARE *pComparison) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetLocate), "This object is in a zombie state"); 416  {
417  ULONG iCurSet, iCurProp;

431  pv->SetProperty(iCurSet, iCurProp, &prop);
432  }
433  }
434  }
435 
436  if(pcCols)
437  *pcCols = pv->m_Columns.m_cColumns;
438  return pv->m_Columns.m_pInfo;

475 // MapClass의 key와 RowClass의 초기화(ReadData 호출) 때문에 override
476 HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::CreateRow(DBROWOFFSET lRowsOffset, DBCOUNTITEM &cRowsObtained, HROW *rgRows)
477 {
478  CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow = NULL;
479  ATLASSERT(lRowsOffset >= 0);
480  CCUBRIDRowsetRow::KeyType key = lRowsOffset+1;
481  ATLASSERT(key > 0);
482  bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup(key,pRow);
483  if (!bFound || pRow == NULL)
484  {
485  DBORDINAL cCols;
486  ATLCOLUMNINFO *pInfo = GetColumnInfo(this, &cCols);
487  ATLTRY(pRow = new CCUBRIDRowsetRow(lRowsOffset, cCols, pInfo, m_spConvert, m_Columns.m_defaultVal))
488  if (pRow == NULL)
489  return E_OUTOFMEMORY;
490 
491  bool bSensitive = false;
492  {
493  CComVariant var;
494  GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_OWNUPDATEDELETE, &var);
495  bSensitive = (V_BOOL(&var)==VARIANT_TRUE);
496  }
497 
498  HRESULT hr = pRow->ReadData(GetRequestHandle(), false, bSensitive);
499  if(FAILED(hr))
500  {
501  delete pRow;
502  pRow = NULL;
503  return hr;
504  }
505 
506  _ATLTRY
507  {
508  m_rgRowHandles.SetAt(key, pRow);
509  }
510  _ATLCATCH( e )
511  {
512  _ATLDELETEEXCEPTION( e );
513  delete pRow;
514  pRow = NULL;
515  return E_OUTOFMEMORY;
516  }
517  }
518  else // found pRow
519  {
520  if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_INVALIDROW)
521  return DB_E_DELETEDROW;
522  }
523  pRow->AddRefRow();
524  m_bReset = false;
525  rgRows[cRowsObtained++] = (HROW)key;
526  return S_OK;
527 }
528 
529 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::AddRefRows(DBCOUNTITEM cRows, const HROW rghRows[],
530  DBREFCOUNT rgRefCounts[], DBROWSTATUS rgRowStatus[])
531 {
532  ClearError();
533  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "This object is in a zombie state");
534  HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::AddRefRows(cRows, rghRows, rgRefCounts, rgRowStatus);
535  if(FAILED(hr))
536  return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset));
537  else
538  return hr;
539 }

541 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetData(HROW hRow, HACCESSOR hAccessor, void *pDstData)
542 {
543  ClearError();
544  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "This object is in a zombie state");
545  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, _T("IRowset::GetData\n"));
546  HRESULT hr;
547  CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow = 0;
548  ATLBINDINGS *pBinding = 0;
549  { // check arguments and prepare data
550  if(hRow==NULL || !m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow) || pRow==NULL)
551  return RaiseError(DB_E_BADROWHANDLE, 0, __uuidof(IRowset));
552  if(!m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding) || pBinding==NULL)
553  return RaiseError(DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE, 0, __uuidof(IRowset));
554  if(pDstData==NULL && pBinding->cBindings!=0)
555  return RaiseError(E_INVALIDARG, 0, __uuidof(IRowset));
556  }
557 
558  if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_INVALIDROW || pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_DELETED)
559  return RaiseError(DB_E_DELETEDROW, 0, __uuidof(IRowset));
560 
561  DBROWCOUNT dwBookmark = pRow->m_iRowset+3;//Util::FindBookmark(m_rgBookmarks, (LONG)pRow->m_iRowset+1);
562 
563  hr = pRow->WriteData(pBinding, pDstData, dwBookmark, this);
564  if(FAILED(hr))
565  return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset));
566  else
567  return hr;
568 }
569 
570 HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::GetNextRowsAsynch(HCHAPTER hReserved, DBROWOFFSET lRowsOffset,
571  DBROWCOUNT cRows, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsObtained, HROW **prghRows)
572 {
573  // TODO: backward fetch 미테스트(아마 잘 안 될듯)
574  // bookmark 미구현
575  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetNextRowsAsynch\n");
576 
577  if(prghRows==NULL || pcRowsObtained==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG;
578  if(cRows==0) return S_OK;
579 
580  if(lRowsOffset<0 && !m_bCanScrollBack)
581  return DB_E_CANTSCROLLBACKWARDS;
582  if(cRows<0 && !m_bCanFetchBack)
583  return DB_E_CANTFETCHBACKWARDS;
584 
585  // In the case where the user is moving backwards after moving forwards,
586  // we do not wrap around to the end of the rowset.
587  if(m_iRowset==0 && !m_bReset && cRows<0)
588  return DB_S_ENDOFROWSET;
589 
590  if(lRowsOffset<0 && m_bReset)
591  return DB_E_CANTSCROLLBACKWARDS; // 아직 데이터가 다 없는데 backward가 가능한가?
592 
593  int iStepSize = ( cRows >= 0 ? 1 : -1 );
594  cRows = AbsVal(cRows); // if cRows==MINLONG_PTR?
595 
596  DBROWOFFSET lTmpRows = lRowsOffset;
597  lRowsOffset += m_iRowset;
598 
599  CComHeapPtr<HROW> rghRowsAllocated;
600  if(*prghRows==NULL)
601  {
602  rghRowsAllocated.Allocate(cRows); // 일단 최대로 잡는다.
603  if(rghRowsAllocated==NULL)
604  return E_OUTOFMEMORY;
605  *prghRows = rghRowsAllocated;
606  }
607 
608  HRESULT hr = S_OK;
609 
610  while(lRowsOffset>=0 && cRows!=0)
611  {
612  // cRows > cRowsInSet && iStepSize < 0
613  if (lRowsOffset == 0 && cRows > 0 && iStepSize < 0)
614  break;
615 
616  hr = CreateRow(lRowsOffset, *pcRowsObtained, *prghRows);
617  if(FAILED(hr))
618  {
619  RefRows(*pcRowsObtained, *prghRows, NULL, NULL, FALSE);
620  for(ULONG iRowDel=0;iRowDel<*pcRowsObtained;iRowDel++)
621  (*prghRows)[iRowDel] = NULL;
622  *pcRowsObtained = 0;
623  return hr;
624  }
625 
626  // TODO: hr==DB_S_ENDOFROWSET이면 다 읽었다는 표시인데
627  // m_bAsynch=false로 바꾸는게 좋을까?
628  // 이 경우 Commit에 의해 다시 테이블을 읽어들일때
629  // 문제가 될지도 모르겠다.
630  if(hr!=S_OK) break;
631 
632  if(m_rgRowData.GetCount()<=(size_t)lRowsOffset)
633  m_rgRowData.SetCount(lRowsOffset+1);
634  if(m_rgBookmarks.GetCount()<=(size_t)lRowsOffset+3)
635  m_rgBookmarks.SetCount(lRowsOffset+4);
636 
637  m_rgBookmarks[lRowsOffset+3] = lRowsOffset+1;
638 
639  cRows--;
640  lRowsOffset += iStepSize;
641  }
642 
643  m_iRowset = lRowsOffset;
644 
645  if(SUCCEEDED(hr) && *pcRowsObtained>0)
646  rghRowsAllocated.Detach();
647  else
648  {
649  if(rghRowsAllocated)
650  *prghRows = 0; // 입력시 *prghRows==NULL이고 에러가 발생했으면 다시 NULL로 만든다.
651  }
652  return hr;
653 }
654 
655 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetNextRows(HCHAPTER hReserved, DBROWOFFSET lRowsOffset,
656  DBROWCOUNT cRows, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsObtained, HROW **prghRows)
657 {
658  ClearError();
659  if(pcRowsObtained) *pcRowsObtained = 0;
660  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "This object is in a zombie state");
661  if(cRows==0) return S_OK;
662  CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowset));
663 
664  if(!m_bExternalFetch)
665  CHECK_CANHOLDROWS(__uuidof(IRowset));
666 
667  if(m_bAsynch)
668  return GetNextRowsAsynch(hReserved, lRowsOffset, cRows, pcRowsObtained, prghRows);
669 
670  bool bProvAlloc = (pcRowsObtained && prghRows && *prghRows==0);
671 
672  HRESULT hr;
673  hr = _RowsetBaseClass::GetNextRows(hReserved, lRowsOffset, cRows, pcRowsObtained, prghRows);
674 
675  if(bProvAlloc && *pcRowsObtained==0)
676  { // ATL Provider Templates의 버그 *prghRows = 0; } if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::ReleaseRows(DBCOUNTITEM cRows, const HROW rghRows[], DBROWOPTIONS rgRowOptions[], DBREFCOUNT rgRefCounts[], DBROWSTATUS rgRowStatus[]) { ClearError(); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::ReleaseRows(cRows, rghRows, rgRowOptions, rgRefCounts, rgRowStatus); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); else return hr; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::RestartPosition(HCHAPTER hReserved) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "This object is in a zombie state"); HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::RestartPosition(hReserved); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset)); cci_fetch_buffer_clear(GetRequestHandle()); if(m_nStatus==2) { hr = Reexecute(); if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "Failed to reexecute the command"); return DB_S_COMMANDREEXECUTED; } return S_OK; } // Provider Templates의 구현은 DELETED 상태인 ROW에 대해 DB_E_DELETEDROW를 반환한다. // spec은 INVALIDROW에 대해서 반환하게 되어 있다. 686 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::ReleaseRows(DBCOUNTITEM cRows, const HROW rghRows[],
687  DBROWOPTIONS rgRowOptions[], DBREFCOUNT rgRefCounts[],
688  DBROWSTATUS rgRowStatus[])
689 {
690  ClearError();
691  HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::ReleaseRows(cRows, rghRows, rgRowOptions, rgRefCounts, rgRowStatus);
692  if(FAILED(hr))
693  return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset));
694  else

698 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::RestartPosition(HCHAPTER hReserved)
699 {
700  ClearError();
701  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "This object is in a zombie state");
702  HRESULT hr = _RowsetBaseClass::RestartPosition(hReserved);
703  if(FAILED(hr))
704  return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowset));
705 
706  cci_fetch_buffer_clear(GetRequestHandle());
707 
708  if(m_nStatus==2)
709  {
710  hr = Reexecute();
711  if(FAILED(hr))
712  return RaiseError(E_FAIL, 1, __uuidof(IRowset), "Failed to reexecute the command");
713  return DB_S_COMMANDREEXECUTED;
714  }
715 
716  return S_OK;
717 }
718 
719 // Provider Templates의 구현은 DELETED 상태인 ROW에 대해 DB_E_DELETEDROW를 반환한다.
720 // spec은 INVALIDROW에 대해서 반환하게 되어 있다.
721 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::IsSameRow(HROW hThisRow, HROW hThatRow)
722 {
723  ClearError();
724  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetIdentity), "This object is in a zombie state");
725  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::IsSameRow\n");
726 
727  // Validate row handles
728  CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow1;
729  if( ! m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((CCUBRIDRowsetRow::KeyType)hThisRow, pRow1) )
730  return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE;
731 
732  CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow2;
733  if( ! m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((CCUBRIDRowsetRow::KeyType)hThatRow, pRow2) )
734  return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE;
735 
736  if (pRow1->m_status == DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW ||
737  pRow2->m_status == DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW)
738  return DB_E_NEWLYINSERTED;
739 
740  if (pRow1->m_status == DBPENDINGSTATUS_INVALIDROW ||
741  pRow2->m_status == DBPENDINGSTATUS_INVALIDROW)
742  return DB_E_DELETEDROW;
743 
744  return pRow1->Compare(pRow2);
745 }

747 HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::OnPropertyChanged(ULONG iCurSet, DBPROP* pDBProp)
748 {
749  HRESULT hr = CUBRIDOnPropertyChanged(this, iCurSet, pDBProp);
750  if(hr==S_FALSE)
751  return _RowsetBaseClass::OnPropertyChanged(iCurSet, pDBProp);
752  else
753  return hr;
754 }

756 HRESULT CCUBRIDRowset::IsValidValue(ULONG iCurSet, DBPROP* pDBProp)
757 {
758  ATLASSERT(pDBProp);
759  if(pDBProp->dwPropertyID==DBPROP_ROWSET_ASYNCH)
760  {
761  // TODO: PREPOPULATE와 POPULATEONDEMAND 둘 다 세팅하는 건 에러겠지?
762  LONG val = V_I4(&pDBProp->vValue);
763  if(val==0 || val==DBPROPVAL_ASYNCH_PREPOPULATE // --> synchronous
764  || val==DBPROPVAL_ASYNCH_POPULATEONDEMAND) // --> asynchronous
765  return S_OK;
766  return S_FALSE;
767  }
768  return _RowsetBaseClass::IsValidValue(iCurSet, pDBProp);
769 }

807 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetRowFromHROW(IUnknown *pUnkOuter, HROW hRow,
808  REFIID riid, IUnknown **ppUnk)
809 {
810  ClearError();
811  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IGetRow), "This object is in a zombie state");
812  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetRowFromHROW\n");
813 
814  DBCOUNTITEM iRowset;
815 
816  { // check arguments
817  CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow = 0;
818  if(hRow==NULL || !m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow) || pRow==NULL)
819  return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE;
820  if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_INVALIDROW
821  || pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_DELETED)
822  return DB_E_DELETEDROW;
823  iRowset = pRow->m_iRowset;
824  }
825 
826  if(!ppUnk)
827  return E_INVALIDARG;
828  if(pUnkOuter && !InlineIsEqualUnknown(riid))
829  return DB_E_NOAGGREGATION;
830 
831  CComPolyObject<CCUBRIDRow> *pRow;
832  HRESULT hr = CComPolyObject<CCUBRIDRow>::CreateInstance(pUnkOuter, &pRow);
833  if(FAILED(hr))
834  return hr;
835 
836  // 생성된 COM 객체를 참조해서, 실패시 자동 해제하도록 한다.
837  CComPtr<IUnknown> spUnk;
838  hr = pRow->QueryInterface(&spUnk);
839  if(FAILED(hr))
840  {
841  delete pRow; // 참조되지 않았기 때문에 수동으로 지운다.
842  return hr;
843  }
844 
845  // Rowset object의 IUnknown을 Row의 Site로 설정한다.
846  CComPtr<IUnknown> spOuterUnk;
847  QueryInterface(__uuidof(IUnknown), (void **)&spOuterUnk);
848  pRow->m_contained.SetSite(spOuterUnk, CCUBRIDRow::FromRowset);
849 
850  CComVariant var;
851  GetPropValue(&DBPROPSET_ROWSET, DBPROP_BOOKMARKS, &var);
852  hr = pRow->m_contained.Initialize(GetRequestHandle(), V_BOOL(&var)==ATL_VARIANT_TRUE, hRow, iRowset);
853  if (FAILED(hr))
854  return E_FAIL;
855 
856  return pRow->QueryInterface(riid, (void **)ppUnk);
857 }
858 
859 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetURLFromHROW(HROW hRow, LPOLESTR *ppwszURL)
860 {
861  ClearError();
862  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetURLFromHROW\n");
863  return RaiseError(DB_E_NOTSUPPORTED, 0, __uuidof(IGetRow));
864 }
865 
866 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::FindNextRow(HCHAPTER hChapter, HACCESSOR hAccessor,
867  void *pFindValue, DBCOMPAREOP CompareOp, DBBKMARK cbBookmark,
868  const BYTE *pBookmark, DBROWOFFSET lRowsOffset, DBROWCOUNT cRows,
869  DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsObtained, HROW **prghRows)
870 {
871  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::FindNextRow\n");
872 
873  ClearError();
874  if(pcRowsObtained) *pcRowsObtained = 0;
875  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetFind), "This object is in a zombie state");
876  CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetFind));
877 
878  if(pcRowsObtained==NULL || prghRows==NULL)
879  return E_INVALIDARG;
880  if(cbBookmark!=0 && pBookmark==NULL)
881  return E_INVALIDARG;
882  if(hChapter!=DB_NULL_HCHAPTER)
883  return DB_E_BADCHAPTER;
884 
885  CHECK_CANHOLDROWS(__uuidof(IRowsetFind));
886 
887  // 바인딩 정보를 구함
888  ATLBINDINGS *pBinding;
889  {
890  // 스펙에 DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE, DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE, E_INVALIDARG를
891  // 반환하는 경우는 정의되어 있지 않지만 해주는게 맞는 것 같다.
892  bool bFound = m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding);
893  if(!bFound || pBinding==NULL)
894  return DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE;
895  if(!(pBinding->dwAccessorFlags & DBACCESSOR_ROWDATA))
896  return DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE; // row accessor 가 아니다.
897  if(pBinding->cBindings!=1)
898  return DB_E_BADBINDINFO;
899  }
900 
901  // 나중에 체크하지만 LTM을 위해 중복
902  {
903  DBCOMPAREOP LocalOp = CompareOp & ~DBCOMPAREOPS_CASESENSITIVE & ~DBCOMPAREOPS_CASEINSENSITIVE;
904  if(LocalOp<0 || LocalOp>DBCOMPAREOPS_NOTCONTAINS)
905  return DB_E_BADCOMPAREOP;
906  if((CompareOp & DBCOMPAREOPS_CASESENSITIVE) && (CompareOp & DBCOMPAREOPS_CASEINSENSITIVE))
907  return DB_E_BADCOMPAREOP;
908  }
909 
910  if(cRows==0 && cbBookmark!=0)
911  return S_OK;
912 
913  DBROWOFFSET iDir = 1;
914  if(cRows<0) { iDir = -1; cRows = -cRows; }
915  if(cRows==0) { iDir = (m_bFindForward?1:-1); }
916 
917  m_bFindForward = (iDir==1);
918 
919  CComHeapPtr<HROW> rghRowsAllocated;
920  if(*prghRows==NULL)
921  {
922  rghRowsAllocated.Allocate(cRows?cRows:1);
923  if(rghRowsAllocated==NULL)
924  return E_OUTOFMEMORY;
925  *prghRows = rghRowsAllocated;
926  }
927 
928  DBROWOFFSET iRowsetTemp = -1;
929  if(cbBookmark!=0)
930  {
931  if(!m_bCanScrollBack)
932  return DB_E_CANTSCROLLBACKWARDS;
933 
934  HRESULT hr = ValidateBookmark(cbBookmark, pBookmark);
935  if(FAILED(hr)) return hr;
936  iRowsetTemp = m_iRowset; // cache the current rowset
937 
938  // 시작 점을 찾는다.
939  if(cbBookmark==1)
940  {
941  if(*pBookmark==DBBMK_FIRST)
942  m_iRowset = 1;
943  else // *pBookmark==DBBMK_LAST
944  m_iRowset = (DBCOUNTITEM)m_rgRowData.GetCount();
945  }
946  else
947  {
948  m_iRowset = m_rgBookmarks[*pBookmark];
949  }
950  if(iDir==1) m_iRowset--;
951  }
952 
953  while(1)
954  {
955  DBCOUNTITEM cTmp;
956  HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[0];
957  m_bExternalFetch = true;
958  HRESULT hr = GetNextRows(hChapter, lRowsOffset, iDir, &cTmp, &phRow);
959  m_bExternalFetch = false;
960  lRowsOffset = 0; // 첫 fetch 때만 lRowsOffset을 적용 if(FAILED(hr) || hr==DB_S_ENDOFROWSET) goto error; // 조건 검사 bool bMatch = true; if(CompareOp!=DBCOMPAREOPS_IGNORE) { CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)*phRow, pRow); ATLASSERT(bFound && pRow!=NULL); } DBBINDING &rBinding = pBinding->pBindings[0]; hr = pRow->Compare(pFindValue, CompareOp, rBinding); if(hr==S_FALSE) bMatch = false; else if(hr!=S_OK) goto error; } if(bMatch) { (*pcRowsObtained)++; break; } else ReleaseRows(1, phRow, NULL, NULL, NULL); continue; error: if(rghRowsAllocated) // 메모리 해제는 자동적으로 이루어진다. *prghRows = 0; if(iRowsetTemp!=-1) m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp; return hr; } if(cRows>1) { // fetch last rows DBCOUNTITEM cTmp; HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[1]; m_bExternalFetch = true; GetNextRows(hChapter, 0, (cRows-1)*iDir, &cTmp, &phRow); // TODO: return value 검사? m_bExternalFetch = false; *pcRowsObtained += cTmp; } else if(cRows==0) { // handle은 반환하지 않고 fetch position만 변경되는 효과를 낸다. HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[0]; ReleaseRows(1, phRow, NULL, NULL, NULL); *pcRowsObtained = 0; if(rghRowsAllocated) // 메모리 해제는 자동적으로 이루어진다. *prghRows = 0; } // bookmark에서 찾기 시작한 경우에는 fetch position을 복구한다. if(iRowsetTemp!=-1) m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp; // prghRows!=NULL이였으면 rghRowsAllocated==NULL // prghRows==NULL이였으면 이미 prghRows==rghRowsAllocated // 따라서 소유권만 없애면 된다. rghRowsAllocated.Detach(); return ( cRows==*pcRowsObtained ? S_OK : DB_S_ENDOFROWSET ); } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData(HCHAPTER hChapter, DBCOUNTITEM cRows, const HROW rghRows[], BOOL fOverWrite, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsRefreshed, HROW **prghRowsRefreshed, DBROWSTATUS **prgRowStatus) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData\n"); ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh)); if(pcRowsRefreshed) *pcRowsRefreshed = 0; if(prghRowsRefreshed) *prghRowsRefreshed = 0; if(prgRowStatus) *prgRowStatus = 0; if(cRows!=0 && rghRows==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; if(pcRowsRefreshed!=NULL && prghRowsRefreshed==NULL) return E_INVALIDARG; DBCOUNTITEM cRowsLocal = ( cRows==0 ? (DBCOUNTITEM)m_rgRowHandles.GetCount() : cRows ); if(cRowsLocal==0) return S_OK; // pcRowsRefreshed!=NULL 이면 HROW와 DBROWSTATUS를 반환한다. // 이 이후로는 메모리를 해제할 일 없음 if(pcRowsRefreshed) { *prghRowsRefreshed = (HROW *)CoTaskMemAlloc(cRowsLocal * sizeof(HROW)); if(*prghRowsRefreshed==0) { return E_OUTOFMEMORY; } if(prgRowStatus) { *prgRowStatus = (DBROWSTATUS *)CoTaskMemAlloc(cRowsLocal * sizeof(DBROWSTATUS)); if(*prgRowStatus==0) { CoTaskMemFree(*prghRowsRefreshed); *prghRowsRefreshed = 0; return E_OUTOFMEMORY; } } *pcRowsRefreshed = cRowsLocal; } DBROWSTATUS statTmp; bool bSucceeded = false, bFailed = false; POSITION pos = m_rgRowHandles.GetStartPosition(); for(DBCOUNTITEM i=0;i<cRowsLocal;i++) { ATLASSERT(pos!=NULL); HROW hRow = ( cRows==0 ? m_rgRowHandles.GetNextKey(pos) : rghRows[i] ); if(pcRowsRefreshed) (*prghRowsRefreshed)[i] = hRow; DBROWSTATUS &rCurStat = ( (pcRowsRefreshed&&prgRowStatus) ? (*prgRowStatus)[i] : statTmp ); CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow); if(!bFound || pRow==NULL) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_INVALID; bFailed = true; continue; } } if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_PENDINGINSERT; bFailed = true; continue; } if(!fOverWrite && (pRow->m_status==0 || pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_UNCHANGED)) { // TODO: 반환값이 정확한 건지 스펙을 보고는 잘 모르겠다. rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_S_OK; bSucceeded = true; continue; } HRESULT hr = pRow->ReadData(GetRequestHandle(), false, true); if(hr==DB_E_DELETEDROW) { rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_DELETED; bFailed = true; continue; } rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_S_OK; bSucceeded = true; } if(!bFailed) return S_OK; else return bSucceeded ? DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED : DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData(HROW hRow, HACCESSOR hAccessor, void *pData) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData\n"); ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh)); // 바인딩 정보를 구함 ATLBINDINGS *pBinding; { bool bFound = m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding); if(!bFound || pBinding==NULL) return DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE; if(!(pBinding->dwAccessorFlags & DBACCESSOR_ROWDATA)) return DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE; // row accessor 가 아니다. if(pData==NULL && pBinding->cBindings!=0) return E_INVALIDARG; } // Attempt to locate the row in our map CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow; { bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow); if(!bFound || pRow==NULL) return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE; } if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW) return DB_E_PENDINGINSERT; DBORDINAL cCols; ATLCOLUMNINFO *pInfo = GetColumnInfo(this, &cCols); DBROWCOUNT dwBookmark = pRow->m_iRowset+3;//Util::FindBookmark(m_rgBookmarks, (LONG)pRow->m_iRowset+1); // 임시 RowClass를 통해 storage에서 데이터를 읽어온 후, pData로 전송한다. CCUBRIDRowsetRow OrigRow(pRow->m_iRowset, cCols, pInfo, m_spConvert, m_Columns.m_defaultVal); OrigRow.ReadData(GetRequestHandle(), false, true); return OrigRow.WriteData(pBinding, pData, dwBookmark); } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::Compare(HCHAPTER hReserved, DBBKMARK cbBookmark1, const BYTE *pBookmark1, DBBKMARK cbBookmark2, const BYTE *pBookmark2, DBCOMPARE *pComparison) { ClearError(); if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetLocate), "This object is in a zombie state"); ClearError(); if(pcRowsObtained) *pcRowsObtained = 0; if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); 964  bool bMatch = true;
965  if(CompareOp!=DBCOMPAREOPS_IGNORE)
966  {
967  CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow;
968  {
969  bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)*phRow, pRow);
970  ATLASSERT(bFound && pRow!=NULL);
971  }
972 
973  DBBINDING &rBinding = pBinding->pBindings[0];
974  hr = pRow->Compare(pFindValue, CompareOp, rBinding);
975  if(hr==S_FALSE)
976  bMatch = false;
977  else if(hr!=S_OK)
978  goto error;
979  }
980 
981  if(bMatch)
982  {
983  (*pcRowsObtained)++;
984  break;
985  }
986  else
987  ReleaseRows(1, phRow, NULL, NULL, NULL);
988  continue;
989 
990 error:
991  if(rghRowsAllocated) // 메모리 해제는 자동적으로 이루어진다.

993  if(iRowsetTemp!=-1)
994  m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp;

996  }

999  { // fetch last rows
1000  DBCOUNTITEM cTmp;
1001  HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[1];
1002  m_bExternalFetch = true;
1003  GetNextRows(hChapter, 0, (cRows-1)*iDir, &cTmp, &phRow); // TODO: return value 검사?
1004  m_bExternalFetch = false;
1005  *pcRowsObtained += cTmp;
1006  }
1007  else if(cRows==0)
1008  { // handle은 반환하지 않고 fetch position만 변경되는 효과를 낸다.
1009  HROW *phRow = &(*prghRows)[0];
1010  ReleaseRows(1, phRow, NULL, NULL, NULL);
1011  *pcRowsObtained = 0;
1012  if(rghRowsAllocated) // 메모리 해제는 자동적으로 이루어진다.
1013  *prghRows = 0;
1014  }
1015 
1016  // bookmark에서 찾기 시작한 경우에는 fetch position을 복구한다.
1017  if(iRowsetTemp!=-1)
1018  m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp;
1019 
1020  // prghRows!=NULL이였으면 rghRowsAllocated==NULL
1021  // prghRows==NULL이였으면 이미 prghRows==rghRowsAllocated
1022  // 따라서 소유권만 없애면 된다.
1023  rghRowsAllocated.Detach();
1024 
1025  return ( cRows==*pcRowsObtained ? S_OK : DB_S_ENDOFROWSET );
1026 }

1028 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData(HCHAPTER hChapter, DBCOUNTITEM cRows,
1029  const HROW rghRows[], BOOL fOverWrite, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsRefreshed,
1030  HROW **prghRowsRefreshed, DBROWSTATUS **prgRowStatus)
1031 {
1032  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::RefreshVisibleData\n");
1033 
1034  ClearError();
1035  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state");
1036  CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh));
1037 
1038  if(pcRowsRefreshed) *pcRowsRefreshed = 0;
1039  if(prghRowsRefreshed) *prghRowsRefreshed = 0;
1040  if(prgRowStatus) *prgRowStatus = 0;
1041 
1042  if(cRows!=0 && rghRows==NULL)
1043  return E_INVALIDARG;
1044  if(pcRowsRefreshed!=NULL && prghRowsRefreshed==NULL)
1045  return E_INVALIDARG;
1046 
1047  DBCOUNTITEM cRowsLocal = ( cRows==0 ? (DBCOUNTITEM)m_rgRowHandles.GetCount() : cRows );
1048  if(cRowsLocal==0)
1049  return S_OK;
1050 
1051  // pcRowsRefreshed!=NULL 이면 HROW와 DBROWSTATUS를 반환한다.
1052  // 이 이후로는 메모리를 해제할 일 없음
1053  if(pcRowsRefreshed)
1054  {
1055  *prghRowsRefreshed = (HROW *)CoTaskMemAlloc(cRowsLocal * sizeof(HROW));
1056  if(*prghRowsRefreshed==0)
1057  {
1058  return E_OUTOFMEMORY;
1059  }
1060 
1061  if(prgRowStatus)
1062  {
1063  *prgRowStatus = (DBROWSTATUS *)CoTaskMemAlloc(cRowsLocal * sizeof(DBROWSTATUS));
1064  if(*prgRowStatus==0)
1065  {
1066  CoTaskMemFree(*prghRowsRefreshed);
1067  *prghRowsRefreshed = 0;
1068  return E_OUTOFMEMORY;
1069  }
1070  }
1071 
1072  *pcRowsRefreshed = cRowsLocal;
1073  }
1074 
1075  DBROWSTATUS statTmp;
1076  bool bSucceeded = false, bFailed = false;
1077  POSITION pos = m_rgRowHandles.GetStartPosition();
1078  for(DBCOUNTITEM i=0;i<cRowsLocal;i++)
1079  {
1080  ATLASSERT(pos!=NULL);
1081 
1082  HROW hRow = ( cRows==0 ? m_rgRowHandles.GetNextKey(pos) : rghRows[i] );
1083  if(pcRowsRefreshed)
1084  (*prghRowsRefreshed)[i] = hRow;
1085  DBROWSTATUS &rCurStat =
1086  ( (pcRowsRefreshed&&prgRowStatus) ? (*prgRowStatus)[i] : statTmp );
1087 
1088  CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow;
1089  {
1090  bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow);
1091  if(!bFound || pRow==NULL)
1092  {
1093  rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_INVALID;
1094  bFailed = true;
1095  continue;
1096  }
1097  }
1098 
1099  if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW)
1100  {
1101  rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_PENDINGINSERT;
1102  bFailed = true;
1103  continue;
1104  }
1105 
1106  if(!fOverWrite && (pRow->m_status==0 || pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_UNCHANGED))
1107  {
1108  // TODO: 반환값이 정확한 건지 스펙을 보고는 잘 모르겠다.
1109  rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_S_OK;
1110  bSucceeded = true;
1111  continue;
1112  }
1113 
1114  HRESULT hr = pRow->ReadData(GetRequestHandle(), false, true);
1115  if(hr==DB_E_DELETEDROW)
1116  {
1117  rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_E_DELETED;
1118  bFailed = true;
1119  continue;
1120  }
1121 
1122  rCurStat = DBROWSTATUS_S_OK;
1123  bSucceeded = true;
1124  }
1125 
1126  if(!bFailed)
1127  return S_OK;
1128  else
1129  return bSucceeded ? DB_S_ERRORSOCCURRED : DB_E_ERRORSOCCURRED;
1130 }

1132 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData(HROW hRow, HACCESSOR hAccessor, void *pData)
1133 {
1134  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetLastVisibleData\n");
1135 
1136  ClearError();
1137  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetRefresh), "This object is in a zombie state");
1138  CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetRefresh));
1139 
1140  // 바인딩 정보를 구함
1141  ATLBINDINGS *pBinding;
1142  {
1143  bool bFound = m_rgBindings.Lookup((ULONG)hAccessor, pBinding);
1144  if(!bFound || pBinding==NULL)
1145  return DB_E_BADACCESSORHANDLE;
1146  if(!(pBinding->dwAccessorFlags & DBACCESSOR_ROWDATA))
1147  return DB_E_BADACCESSORTYPE; // row accessor 가 아니다.
1148  if(pData==NULL && pBinding->cBindings!=0)
1149  return E_INVALIDARG;
1150  }
1151 
1152  // Attempt to locate the row in our map
1153  CCUBRIDRowsetRow *pRow;
1154  {
1155  bool bFound = m_rgRowHandles.Lookup((ULONG)hRow, pRow);
1156  if(!bFound || pRow==NULL)
1157  return DB_E_BADROWHANDLE;
1158  }
1159 
1160  if(pRow->m_status==DBPENDINGSTATUS_NEW)
1161  return DB_E_PENDINGINSERT;
1162

1164  ATLCOLUMNINFO *pInfo = GetColumnInfo(this, &cCols);
1165  DBROWCOUNT dwBookmark = pRow->m_iRowset+3;//Util::FindBookmark(m_rgBookmarks, (LONG)pRow->m_iRowset+1);
1166 
1167  // 임시 RowClass를 통해 storage에서 데이터를 읽어온 후, pData로 전송한다.
1168  CCUBRIDRowsetRow OrigRow(pRow->m_iRowset, cCols, pInfo, m_spConvert, m_Columns.m_defaultVal);
1169  OrigRow.ReadData(GetRequestHandle(), false, true);
1170  return OrigRow.WriteData(pBinding, pData, dwBookmark);
1171 }

1225  DBHASHVALUE rgHashedValues[], DBROWSTATUS rgBookmarkStatus[])

1227  ClearError();
1228  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetLocate), "This object is in a zombie state");

1237 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetApproximatePosition(HCHAPTER hReserved, DBBKMARK cbBookmark,
1238  const BYTE *pBookmark, DBCOUNTITEM *pulPosition, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRows)
1239 {
1240  ClearError();
1241  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll), "This object is in a zombie state");
1242  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetApproximatePosition\n");
1243 
1244  DBCOUNTITEM ulRowCount = (DBCOUNTITEM)m_rgRowData.GetCount();
1245 
1246  if(cbBookmark==0 || pulPosition==NULL)
1247  {
1248  // 밑에도 있지만, 에러가 생겼을 경우 *pcRows값이 바뀌면 // 안되므로 따로 쓴다. if(pcRows) *pcRows = ulRowCount; return S_OK; // return only total number of rows } HRESULT hr = ValidateBookmark(cbBookmark, pBookmark); if(hr!=S_OK) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); if(cbBookmark!=1 && m_rgBookmarks[*pBookmark]==-1) // 삭제된 bookmark return RaiseError(DB_E_BADBOOKMARK, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); if(pcRows) *pcRows = ulRowCount; if(m_rgRowData.GetCount()==0) { *pulPosition = 0; } else if(cbBookmark==1) { if(*pBookmark==DBBMK_FIRST) *pulPosition=1; else // *pBookmark==DBBMK_LAST *pulPosition=ulRowCount; } else { *pulPosition = m_rgBookmarks[*pBookmark]; } return S_OK; } STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetRowsAtRatio(HWATCHREGION hReserved1, HCHAPTER hReserved2, DBCOUNTITEM ulNumerator, DBCOUNTITEM ulDenominator, DBROWCOUNT cRows, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsObtained, HROW **prghRows) { ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetRowsAtRatio\n"); ClearError(); if(pcRowsObtained) *pcRowsObtained = 0; if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll), "This object is in a zombie state"); CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); CHECK_CANHOLDROWS(__uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); // 인자 검사 if(pcRowsObtained==NULL || prghRows==NULL) return RaiseError(E_INVALIDARG, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); if(ulDenominator==0 || ulNumerator>ulDenominator) return RaiseError(DB_E_BADRATIO, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); // Rowset의 끝 if( (ulNumerator==0 && cRows<0) || (ulNumerator==ulDenominator && cRows>0) ) return RaiseError(DB_S_ENDOFROWSET, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); DBROWOFFSET iRowsetTemp = m_iRowset; // Cache the current rowset // 시작 점을 찾는다. DBCOUNTITEM ulRowCount = (DBCOUNTITEM)m_rgRowData.GetCount(); if(ulNumerator==0) m_iRowset = 0; else if(ulNumerator==ulDenominator) m_iRowset = ulRowCount; else m_iRowset = ulNumerator * ulRowCount / ulDenominator; // 여기서 실제로 handle을 생성한다. m_bExternalFetch = true; HRESULT hr = GetNextRows(hReserved2, 0, cRows, pcRowsObtained, prghRows); m_bExternalFetch = false; m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp; if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetLocate)); else return hr; }
1249  // 안되므로 따로 쓴다.
1250  if(pcRows) *pcRows = ulRowCount;
1251  return S_OK; // return only total number of rows
1252  }
1253 
1254  HRESULT hr = ValidateBookmark(cbBookmark, pBookmark);
1255  if(hr!=S_OK)
1256  return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll));
1257 
1258  if(cbBookmark!=1 && m_rgBookmarks[*pBookmark]==-1) // 삭제된 bookmark
1259  return RaiseError(DB_E_BADBOOKMARK, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll));
1260 
1261  if(pcRows)
1262  *pcRows = ulRowCount;
1263 
1264  if(m_rgRowData.GetCount()==0)
1265  {
1266  *pulPosition = 0;
1267  }
1268  else if(cbBookmark==1)
1269  {
1270  if(*pBookmark==DBBMK_FIRST)
1271  *pulPosition=1;
1272  else // *pBookmark==DBBMK_LAST
1273  *pulPosition=ulRowCount;
1274  }
1275  else
1276  {
1277  *pulPosition = m_rgBookmarks[*pBookmark];
1278  }
1279 
1280  return S_OK;
1281 }

1283 STDMETHODIMP CCUBRIDRowset::GetRowsAtRatio(HWATCHREGION hReserved1, HCHAPTER hReserved2,
1284  DBCOUNTITEM ulNumerator, DBCOUNTITEM ulDenominator,
1285  DBROWCOUNT cRows, DBCOUNTITEM *pcRowsObtained, HROW **prghRows)
1286 {
1287  ATLTRACE(atlTraceDBProvider, 2, "CCUBRIDRowset::GetRowsAtRatio\n");
1288 
1289  ClearError();
1290  if(pcRowsObtained) *pcRowsObtained = 0;
1291  if(m_nStatus==1) return RaiseError(E_UNEXPECTED, 1, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll), "This object is in a zombie state");
1292  CHECK_RESTART(__uuidof(IRowsetScroll));
1293 
1294  CHECK_CANHOLDROWS(__uuidof(IRowsetScroll));
1295 
1296  // 인자 검사 if(pcRowsObtained==NULL || prghRows==NULL) return RaiseError(E_INVALIDARG, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); if(ulDenominator==0 || ulNumerator>ulDenominator) return RaiseError(DB_E_BADRATIO, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); // Rowset의 끝 if( (ulNumerator==0 && cRows<0) || (ulNumerator==ulDenominator && cRows>0) ) return RaiseError(DB_S_ENDOFROWSET, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll)); DBROWOFFSET iRowsetTemp = m_iRowset; // Cache the current rowset // 시작 점을 찾는다. DBCOUNTITEM ulRowCount = (DBCOUNTITEM)m_rgRowData.GetCount(); if(ulNumerator==0) m_iRowset = 0; else if(ulNumerator==ulDenominator) m_iRowset = ulRowCount; else m_iRowset = ulNumerator * ulRowCount / ulDenominator; // 여기서 실제로 handle을 생성한다. m_bExternalFetch = true; HRESULT hr = GetNextRows(hReserved2, 0, cRows, pcRowsObtained, prghRows); m_bExternalFetch = false; m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp; if(FAILED(hr)) return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetLocate)); else return hr; }
1297  if(pcRowsObtained==NULL || prghRows==NULL)
1298  return RaiseError(E_INVALIDARG, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll));
1299  if(ulDenominator==0 || ulNumerator>ulDenominator)
1300  return RaiseError(DB_E_BADRATIO, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll));
1301 
1302  // Rowset의 끝
1303  if( (ulNumerator==0 && cRows<0) || (ulNumerator==ulDenominator && cRows>0) )
1304  return RaiseError(DB_S_ENDOFROWSET, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetScroll));
1305 
1306  DBROWOFFSET iRowsetTemp = m_iRowset; // Cache the current rowset
1307 
1308  // 시작 점을 찾는다.
1309  DBCOUNTITEM ulRowCount = (DBCOUNTITEM)m_rgRowData.GetCount();
1310  if(ulNumerator==0)
1311  m_iRowset = 0;
1312  else if(ulNumerator==ulDenominator)
1313  m_iRowset = ulRowCount;
1314  else
1315  m_iRowset = ulNumerator * ulRowCount / ulDenominator;
1316 
1317  // 여기서 실제로 handle을 생성한다.
1318  m_bExternalFetch = true;
1319  HRESULT hr = GetNextRows(hReserved2, 0, cRows, pcRowsObtained, prghRows);
1320  m_bExternalFetch = false;
1321 
1322  m_iRowset = iRowsetTemp;
1323 
1324  if(FAILED(hr))
1325  return RaiseError(hr, 0, __uuidof(IRowsetLocate));
1326  else
1327  return hr;
1328 }
